<script type="text/javascript">
    var notFoundValue = 'not_found';

    //Function to capture Adobe Id
    function getAdobeVisitorID() {
        try {
            return Visitor.getInstance("5EC33EEF53EB80820A490D44@AdobeOrg").getMarketingCloudVisitorID();
        } catch (e) {
            return false;
        }
    }

    //Function to first look in the Invoca cookie for the Adobe ID else fallback to function above
    function getExistingAdobeVisitorId() {
        return Invoca.Tools.readInvocaData('s_vi', getAdobeVisitorID());
    }

    //Get Universal Analytics ID and Default Campaign Id
    function getExistingClientId() {
        // If ga is defined, check for the clientId and return it
        if (typeof ga !== 'undefined' && typeof ga.getAll === 'function') {
            var clientId = ga.getAll()[0].get('clientId');
            return clientId;

            // otherwise, return false so waitFor knows to try again for defined wait time
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    }

    function getSizmekParams() {
        if (typeof SZCD !== "undefined") {
            var szcdUid = SZCD.UID || notFoundValue;
            var szcdCid = SZCD.CID || notFoundValue;
            var szcdLid = SZCD.LID || notFoundValue;
        } else {
            var szcdUid = szcdCid = szcdLid = notFoundValue;
        }

        return {
            UID: szcdUid,
            CID: szcdCid,
            LID: szcdLid
        };
    }

    //Function to confirm both variables have been captured before running Invoca script
    function cookieParams() {
        var adobeVisitorId = getExistingAdobeVisitorId();
        var clientId = getExistingClientId();
        return (adobeVisitorId && clientId) ? [adobeVisitorId, clientId] : false;
    }

    //Wait for 1 second to capture Google Client Id
    Invoca.Tools.waitFor(cookieParams, function (params) {
        var adobeId = params[0] || getExistingAdobeVisitorId() || notFoundValue;
        var invocaGcid = params[1] || getExistingClientId() || notFoundValue;
        var szcdUid = getSizmekParams().UID || notFoundValue;
        var szcdCid = getSizmekParams().CID || notFoundValue;
        var szcdLid = getSizmekParams().LID || notFoundValue;


        // Creates the default Invoca campaign ID if invsrc parameter is NOT in the URL
        function createFallBackId() {
            var invocaCampaignId = Invoca.Tools.parseReferrer({
                "google.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "bing.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "yahoo.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "ask.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "aol.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "wow.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "blekko.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "baidu.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "info.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "webcrawler.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "infospace.com": "resi_cross_region_natural",
                "facebook.com": "resi_cross_region_social",
                "twitter.com": "resi_cross_region_social",
                "linkedin.com": "resi_cross_region_social",
                "<referringDomain>": "<campaignId>",             // Example if list is ever augmented
                "": "resi_cross_region_direct"
            }, "resi_cross_region_referral", null, 'topLevelDomain');

            return invocaCampaignId;
        }

        //Reads existing default ID, if available
        function findFallbackId() {
            var data = Invoca.Tools.readCookie("invoca_default_id");

            if (data) {
                var theData = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(data));
                if (theData.default_id) {
                    return theData.default_id;
                }
            }
            return null;
        }

        //Read existing default id or create new default id
        function getFallbackId() {
            var id = findFallbackId();

            if (!id) {
                id = createFallBackId();
                var data = { default_id: id };
                data = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(data));

                Invoca.Tools.setCookie("invoca_default_id", data, 1);
            }
            return id;
        }

        var fallback = getFallbackId();

        //Invoca Data Storage
        var invocaParams = {
            s_vi: adobeId,
            ua: Invoca.Tools.readInvocaData("ua", window.navigator.userAgent),
            referrer: Invoca.Tools.readInvocaData("referrer", document.referrer),
            g_cid: invocaGcid,
            current_url: window.location.href.split('?')[0],
            sz_uid: szcdUid,
            sz_cid: szcdCid,
            sz_lid: szcdLid
        }

        //(Html.Sitecore().CurrentItem).Fields["InvocaCSSSpanName"].Value
        // Custom logic added by Frontier.
        //The class name they use for the numberSelector is different between their Shop and Offer pages.
        //The custom logic checks if 1.) the pages should swap a invoca phone number and 2.) that the page has a numberSelector class name
        var InvocaCSSTrackToggle = '1';
        var InvocaCSSSpanName = 'InvocaSpanClass';
        if (InvocaCSSTrackToggle.toString() == "1" && InvocaCSSSpanName.toString().length > 0) {
            //Invoca Number Placing Function
            Invoca.PNAPI.integration({
                networkId: 1171,
                numberSelector: "." + InvocaCSSSpanName, //Make sure to fill this string in with the span class of the phone number location
                campaignIdOverrideParam: "invsrc",
                defaultCampaignId: fallback,
                poolParams: invocaParams,
                cookieDays: 1                           //set to 1 Day
            });
        }
    }, [null, null], 1000)
</script>
<!--Invoca Code Ends-->

<script type="text/javascript">
    // GET COOKIE
    function getCookie(name) {
        var pattern = RegExp(name + "=.[^;]*")
        matched = document.cookie.match(pattern)
        if (matched) {
            var cookie = matched[0].split('=')
            return cookie[1]
        }
        return false
    }
    </script>

                function evar49Function() {
                  var geoData = getCookie('GeolocationData');
                  var parsedGeoData = JSON.parse(geoData);
                  if (parsedGeoData.iconColor == "green")
